# rocSOLVER LAPACK-like functions[#](#rocsolver-lapack-like-functions)

Other LAPACK-like routines are provided by rocSOLVER. They are divided into the following subcategories:

[Triangular factorizations](#liketriangular): Based on Gaussian elimination.[Linear-systems solvers](#likelinears): Based on triangular factorizations.[Symmetric eigensolvers](#likeeigens): Eigenproblems for symmetric matrices.[Singular value decomposition](#likesvds): Singular values and related problems for general matrices.

Note

The API descriptions use the following notations:

`i`

,`j`

, and`k`

are used as general purpose indices. In some legacy LAPACK APIs,`k`

can be a parameter indicating some problem or matrix dimension.Depending on the context, when it is necessary to index rows, columns, and blocks or submatrices,

`i`

is assigned to rows,`j`

to columns, and`k`

to blocks.`l`

is always used to index matrices or problems in a batch.`x[i]`

stands for the i-th element of vector x, while`A[i,j]`

represents the element in the i-th row and j-th column of matrix`A`

. Indices are 1-based, for instance,`x[1]`

is the first element of`x`

.To identify a block in a matrix or a matrix in the batch,

`k`

and`l`

are used as sub-indices`x_i`

\(=x_i\). Both notations are used, \(x_i\) when displaying mathematical equations and`x_i`

in the text describing the function parameters.If

`X`

is a real vector or matrix, \(X^T\) indicates its transpose. If`X`

is complex, then \(X^H\) represents its conjugate transpose. When`X`

could be real or complex, the descriptions use`X'`

to indicate`X`

transposed or`X`

conjugate transposed, accordingly.When a matrix

`A`

is formed as the product of several matrices, the following notation is used:`A=M(1)M(2)...M(t)`

.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv421rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv421rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GETF2_NPVT computes the LU factorization of a general m-by-n matrix A without partial pivoting.

(This is the unblocked Level-2-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with small and mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization has the form

\[ A = LU \]where L is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and U is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note

Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK API

[GETF2](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a028df88a6b2ae495b6fdcc4aa3321985)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the m-by-n matrix A to be factored. On exit, the factors L and U from the factorization. The unit diagonal elements of L are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, U is singular. U[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cgetf2_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_cgetf2_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETF2_NPVT_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of general m-by-n matrices without partial pivoting.

(This is the unblocked Level-2-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with small and mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch has the form

\[ A_l = L_lU_l \]where \(L_l\) is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and \(U_l\) is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note

Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK API

[GETF2_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1acbab7dd1189d9c3f8a9c4652d453d514)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of all matrices A_l in the batch.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the m-by-n matrices A_l to be factored. On exit, the factors L_l and U_l from the factorizations. The unit diagonal elements of L_l are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_64([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const int64_t m, const int64_t n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const int64_t lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, int64_t *info, const int64_t batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_6414rocblas_handleK7int64_tK7int64_tP22rocblas_double_complexK7int64_tK14rocblas_strideP7int64_tK7int64_t)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_64([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const int64_t m, const int64_t n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const int64_t lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, int64_t *info, const int64_t batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_cgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_6414rocblas_handleK7int64_tK7int64_tP21rocblas_float_complexK7int64_tK14rocblas_strideP7int64_tK7int64_t)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_64([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const int64_t m, const int64_t n, double *A, const int64_t lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, int64_t *info, const int64_t batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_strided_batched_6414rocblas_handleK7int64_tK7int64_tPdK7int64_tK14rocblas_strideP7int64_tK7int64_t)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv437rocsolver_zgetf2_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv437rocsolver_dgetf2_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv437rocsolver_sgetf2_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETF2_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of general m-by-n matrices without partial pivoting.

(This is the unblocked Level-2-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with small and mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch has the form

\[ A_l = L_lU_l \]where \(L_l\) is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and \(U_l\) is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note

Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK-like API

[GETF2_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a3c64b17aada5327298b42798eca15ce5)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of all matrices A_l in the batch.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the m-by-n matrices A_l to be factored. On exit, the factors L_l and U_l from the factorization. The unit diagonal elements of L_l are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetrf_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv421rocsolver_dgetrf_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv421rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GETRF_NPVT computes the LU factorization of a general m-by-n matrix A without partial pivoting.

(This is the blocked Level-3-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization has the form

\[ A = LU \]where L is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and U is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note: Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK-like API

[GETRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a75c831efc81b0f80f726d71a79d31b91)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of the matrix A.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the m-by-n matrix A to be factored. On exit, the factors L and U from the factorization. The unit diagonal elements of L are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, U is singular. U[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgetrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_zgetrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_dgetrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRF_NPVT_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of general m-by-n matrices without partial pivoting.

(This is the blocked Level-3-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch has the form

\[ A_l = L_lU_l \]where \(L_l\) is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and \(U_l\) is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note: Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK-like API

[GETRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1afaaeb3de3f891c4b2b3bb0925abce18a)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of all matrices A_l in the batch.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the m-by-n matrices A_l to be factored. On exit, the factors L_l and U_l from the factorizations. The unit diagonal elements of L_l are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)m, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv437rocsolver_sgetrf_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of general m-by-n matrices without partial pivoting.

(This is the blocked Level-3-BLAS version of the algorithm. An optimized internal implementation without rocBLAS calls could be executed with mid-size matrices if optimizations are enabled (default option). For more details, see the “Tuning rocSOLVER performance” section of the Library Design Guide).

The factorization of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch has the form

\[ A_l = L_lU_l \]where \(L_l\) is lower triangular with unit diagonal elements (lower trapezoidal if m > n), and \(U_l\) is upper triangular (upper trapezoidal if m < n).

Note: Although this routine can offer better performance, Gaussian elimination without pivoting is not backward stable. If numerical accuracy is compromised, use the legacy-LAPACK-like API

[GETRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ae0feab0135a20479c7bb954b3348261d)routines instead.- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**m**–**[in]**rocblas_int. m >= 0. The number of rows of all matrices A_l in the batch.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the m-by-n matrices A_l to be factored. On exit, the factors L_l and U_l from the factorization. The unit diagonal elements of L_l are not stored.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= m. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero element in the diagonal. The factorization from this point might be incomplete.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cgeblttrf_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_cgeblttrf_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRF_NPVT computes the LU factorization of a block tridiagonal matrix without partial pivoting.

The LU factorization of a block tridiagonal matrix

\[\begin{split} M = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_1 & C_1\\ A_1 & B_2 & C_2\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{n-2} & B_{n-1} & C_{n-1}\\ & & & A_{n-1} & B_n \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]with \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, can be represented as

\[\begin{split} M = \left[\begin{array}{cccc} L_1 \\ A_1 & L_2\\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{n-1} & L_n \end{array}\right] \left[\begin{array}{cccc} I & U_1 \\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & I & U_{n-1}\\ & & & I \end{array}\right] = LU \end{split}\]where the blocks \(L_i\) and \(U_i\) are also general blocks of size nb.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of the matrix.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks A_i arranged one after the other.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_i.**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*nb*nblocks. On entry, contains the blocks B_i arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks L_i in factorized form as returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c)**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_i.**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*nb*(nblocks-1). On entry, contains the blocks C_i arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks U_i.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_i.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, the matrix is singular.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgeblttrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_zgeblttrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cgeblttrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_cgeblttrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRF_NPVT_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of block tridiagonal matrices without partial pivoting.

The LU factorization of a block tridiagonal matrix \(M_l\) in the batch

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{l1}\\ A_{l1} & B_{l2} & C_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(l-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]with \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, can be represented as

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{cccc} L_{l1} \\ A_{l1} & L_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-1)} & L_{ln} \end{array}\right] \left[\begin{array}{cccc} I & U_{l1} \\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & I & U_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & I \end{array}\right] = L_lU_l \end{split}\]where the blocks \(L_{li}\) and \(U_{li}\) are also general blocks of size nb.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**A**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks A_{li} arranged one after the other.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}.**B**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*nb*nblocks. On entry, contains the blocks B_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks L_{li} in factorized form as returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c)**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_{li}.**C**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldc*nb*(nblocks-1). On entry, contains the blocks C_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks U_{li}.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_{li}.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of l-th batch instance. If info[l] = i > 0, the l-th batch instance is singular.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_dgeblttrf_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of block tridiagonal matrices without partial pivoting.

The LU factorization of a block tridiagonal matrix \(M_l\) in the batch

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{l1}\\ A_{l1} & B_{l2} & C_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]with \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, can be represented as

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{cccc} L_{l1} \\ A_{l1} & L_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-1)} & L_{ln} \end{array}\right] \left[\begin{array}{cccc} I & U_{l1} \\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & I & U_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & I \end{array}\right] = L_lU_l \end{split}\]where the blocks \(L_{li}\) and \(U_{li}\) are also general blocks of size nb.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). Contains the blocks A_{li} arranged one after the other.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block A_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance A_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*nb*nblocks.**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). On entry, contains the blocks B_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks L_{li} in factorized form as returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c)**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix blocks B_{li}.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use case is strideB >= ldb*nb*nblocks.**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). On entry, contains the blocks C_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks U_{li}.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix blocks C_{li}.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use case is strideC >= ldc*nb*nblocks.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of l-th batch instance. If info[l] = i > 0, the l-th batch instance is singular.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_interleaved_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)inca, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incc, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv444rocsolver_sgeblttrf_npvt_interleaved_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRF_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED computes the LU factorization of a batch of block tridiagonal matrices without partial pivoting.

The LU factorization of a block tridiagonal matrix \(M_l\) in the batch

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{l1}\\ A_{l1} & B_{l2} & C_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right] \end{split}\]with \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, can be represented as

\[\begin{split} M_l = \left[\begin{array}{cccc} L_{l1} \\ A_{l1} & L_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-1)} & L_{ln} \end{array}\right] \left[\begin{array}{cccc} I & U_{l1} \\ & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & I & U_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & I \end{array}\right] = L_lU_l \end{split}\]where the blocks \(L_{li}\) and \(U_{li}\) are also general blocks of size nb.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). Contains the blocks A_{li} arranged one after the other.**inca**–**[in]**rocblas_int. inca > 0. Stride from the start of one row of A_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are inca = 1 (strided batched case) or inca = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= inca * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of A_{li} to the next.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block A_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance A_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use cases are strideA >= lda*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideA = 1 (interleaved batched case).**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). On entry, contains the blocks B_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks L_{li} in factorized form as returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c)**incb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incb > 0. Stride from the start of one row of B_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are incb = 1 (strided batched case) or incb = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= incb * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of B_{li} to the next.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use cases are strideB >= ldb*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideB = 1 (interleaved batched case).**C**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). On entry, contains the blocks C_{li} arranged one after the other. On exit it is overwritten by blocks U_{li}.**incc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incc > 0. Stride from the start of one row of C_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are incc = 1 (strided batched case) or incc = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= incc * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of C_{li} to the next.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use cases are strideC >= ldc*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideC = 1 (interleaved batched case).**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for factorization of l-th batch instance. If info[l] = i > 0, the l-th batch instance is singular.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv421rocsolver_sgetri_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT inverts a general n-by-n matrix A using the LU factorization computed by

[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c).The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A^{-1}L = U^{-1} \]where L is the lower triangular factor of A with unit diagonal elements, and U is the upper triangular factor.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the factors L and U of the factorization A = L*U returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c). On exit, the inverse of A if info = 0; otherwise undefined.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, U is singular. U[i,i] is the first zero pivot.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv429rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT_BATCHED inverts a batch of general n-by-n matrices using the LU factorization computed by

[GETRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a43633a8e6af68edd0a8854c07fbebd4b).The inverse of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l^{-1} L_l^{} = U_l^{-1} \]where \(L_l\) is the lower triangular factor of \(A_l\) with unit diagonal elements, and \(U_l\) is the upper triangular factor.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a43633a8e6af68edd0a8854c07fbebd4b). On exit, the inverses of A_l if info[l] = 0; otherwise undefined.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv437rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED inverts a batch of general n-by-n matrices using the LU factorization computed by

[GETRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a00220768aedbc9e13638ad7fdff18710).The inverse of matrix \(A_l\) in the batch is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l^{-1} L_l^{} = U_l^{-1} \]where \(L_l\) is the lower triangular factor of \(A_l\) with unit diagonal elements, and \(U_l\) is the upper triangular factor.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a00220768aedbc9e13638ad7fdff18710). On exit, the inverses of A_l if info[l] = 0; otherwise undefined.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgetri_outofplace([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv427rocsolver_dgetri_outofplace14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv427rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GETRI_OUTOFPLACE computes the inverse \(C = A^{-1}\) of a general n-by-n matrix A.

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ AC = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and A is factorized as \(A = PLU\) as given by

[GETRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a75c831efc81b0f80f726d71a79d31b91).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. The factors L and U of the factorization A = P*L*U returned by[GETRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a75c831efc81b0f80f726d71a79d31b91).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The pivot indices returned by[GETRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a75c831efc81b0f80f726d71a79d31b91).**C**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. If info = 0, the inverse of A. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, U is singular. U[i,i] is the first zero pivot.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideP, float *const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv435rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_OUTOFPLACE_BATCHED computes the inverse \(C_l = A_l^{-1}\) of a batch of general n-by-n matrices \(A_l\).

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l C_l = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and \(A_l\) is factorized as \(A_l = P_l L_l U_l\) as given by

[GETRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1afaaeb3de3f891c4b2b3bb0925abce18a).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. The factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = P_l*L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1afaaeb3de3f891c4b2b3bb0925abce18a).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideP). The pivot indices returned by[GETRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1afaaeb3de3f891c4b2b3bb0925abce18a).**strideP**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector ipiv_l to the next one ipiv_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideP. Normal use case is strideP >= n.**C**–**[out]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. If info[l] = 0, the inverse of matrices A_l. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cgetri_outofplace_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideP,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv443rocsolver_cgetri_outofplace_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*ipiv, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideP, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv443rocsolver_sgetri_outofplace_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_OUTOFPLACE_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the inverse \(C_l = A_l^{-1}\) of a batch of general n-by-n matrices \(A_l\).

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l C_l = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and \(A_l\) is factorized as \(A_l = P_l L_l U_l\) as given by

[GETRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ae0feab0135a20479c7bb954b3348261d).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). The factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = P_l*L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ae0feab0135a20479c7bb954b3348261d).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n**ipiv**–**[in]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideP). The pivot indices returned by[GETRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1ae0feab0135a20479c7bb954b3348261d).**strideP**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector ipiv_l to the next one ipiv_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideP. Normal use case is strideP >= n.**C**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). If info[l] = 0, the inverse of matrices A_l. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C_l.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix C_l to the next one C_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use case is strideC >= ldc*n**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT_OUTOFPLACE computes the inverse \(C = A^{-1}\) of a general n-by-n matrix A without partial pivoting.

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ AC = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and A is factorized as \(A = LU\) as given by

[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of the matrix A.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. The factors L and U of the factorization A = L*U returned by[GETRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a86178c8a92913cb86f1169fa1db7fa6c).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**C**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. If info = 0, the inverse of A. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, U is singular. U[i,i] is the first zero pivot.
