[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT_OUTOFPLACE_BATCHED computes the inverse \(C_l^{} = A_l^{-1}\) of a batch of general n-by-n matrices \(A_l\) without partial pivoting.

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l C_l = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and \(A_l\) is factorized as \(A_l = L_l U_l\) as given by

[GETRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a43633a8e6af68edd0a8854c07fbebd4b).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. The factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a43633a8e6af68edd0a8854c07fbebd4b).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**C**–**[out]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldc*n. If info[l] = 0, the inverse of matrices A_l. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv448rocsolver_sgetri_npvt_outofplace_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GETRI_NPVT_OUTOFPLACE_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the inverse \(C_l^{} = A_l^{-1}\) of a batch of general n-by-n matrices \(A_l\) without partial pivoting.

The inverse is computed by solving the linear system

\[ A_l C_l = I \]where I is the identity matrix, and \(A_l\) is factorized as \(A_l = L_l U_l\) as given by

[GETRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a00220768aedbc9e13638ad7fdff18710).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The number of rows and columns of all matrices A_l in the batch.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). The factors L_l and U_l of the factorization A_l = L_l*U_l returned by[GETRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a00220768aedbc9e13638ad7fdff18710).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n**C**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). If info[l] = 0, the inverse of matrices A_l. Otherwise, undefined.**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of C_l.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix C_l to the next one C_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use case is strideC >= ldc*n**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for inversion of A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, U_l is singular. U_l[i,i] is the first zero pivot.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgeblttrs_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, double *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_dgeblttrs_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, float *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRS_NPVT solves a system of linear equations given by a block tridiagonal matrix in its factorized form (without partial pivoting).

The linear system has the form

\[\begin{split} MX = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_1 & C_1\\ A_1 & B_2 & C_2\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{n-2} & B_{n-1} & C_{n-1}\\ & & & A_{n-1} & B_n \end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{c} X_1\\ X_2\\ X_3\\ \vdots\\ X_n \end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c} R_1\\ R_2\\ R_3\\ \vdots\\ R_n \end{array}\right]=R \end{split}\]where matrix M has \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, and the right-hand-side blocks \(R_i\) are general blocks of size nb-by-nrhs. The blocks of matrix M should be in the factorized form as returned by

[GEBLTTRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a899cab4f1ff90f590b386d16d6818379).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of the matrix.**nrhs**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nrhs >= 0. The number of right hand sides, i.e., the number of columns of blocks R_i.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks A_i as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a899cab4f1ff90f590b386d16d6818379).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_i.**B**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*nb*nblocks. Contains the blocks B_i as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a899cab4f1ff90f590b386d16d6818379).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_i.**C**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldc*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks C_i as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a899cab4f1ff90f590b386d16d6818379).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_i.**X**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldx*nblocks*nrhs. On entry, X contains the right-hand-side blocks R_i. It is overwritten by solution vectors X_i on exit.**ldx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldx >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks X_i.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *const C[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, float *const X[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRS_NPVT_BATCHED solves a batch of system of linear equations given by block tridiagonal matrices in its factorized form (without partial pivoting).

Each linear system has the form

\[\begin{split} M_lX_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{l1}\\ A_{l1} & B_{l2} & C_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{c} X_{l1}\\ X_{l2}\\ X_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ X_{ln} \end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c} R_{l1}\\ R_{l2}\\ R_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ R_{ln} \end{array}\right]=R_l \end{split}\]where matrix \(M_l\) has \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, and the right-hand-side blocks \(R_{li}\) are general blocks of size nb-by-nrhs. The blocks of matrix \(M_l\) should be in the factorized form as returned by

[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a61577fc6910e8793b34d4903fbfad088).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**nrhs**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nrhs >= 0. The number of right hand sides, i.e., the number of columns of blocks R_{li}.**A**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks A_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a61577fc6910e8793b34d4903fbfad088).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}.**B**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*nb*nblocks. Contains the blocks B_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a61577fc6910e8793b34d4903fbfad088).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_{li}.**C**–**[in]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldc*nb*(nblocks-1). Contains the blocks C_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a61577fc6910e8793b34d4903fbfad088).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_{li}.**X**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldx*nblocks*nrhs. On entry, X contains the right-hand-side blocks R_{li}. It is overwritten by solution vectors X_{li} on exit.**ldx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldx >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks X_{li}.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zgeblttrs_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, -
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC, float *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideX, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv440rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRS_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED solves a batch of system of linear equations given by block tridiagonal matrices in its factorized form (without partial pivoting).

Each linear system has the form

\[\begin{split} M_lX_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{l1}\\ A_{l1} & B_{l2} & C_{l2}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{c} X_{l1}\\ X_{l2}\\ X_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ X_{ln} \end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c} R_{l1}\\ R_{l2}\\ R_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ R_{ln} \end{array}\right]=R_l \end{split}\]where matrix \(M_l\) has \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, and the right-hand-side blocks \(R_{li}\) are general blocks of size nb-by-nrhs. The blocks of matrix \(M_l\) should be in the factorized form as returned by

[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a114ea0d398c1940f1cb493cc8be2f1f6).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**nrhs**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nrhs >= 0. The number of right hand sides, i.e., the number of columns of blocks R_{li}.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). Contains the blocks A_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a114ea0d398c1940f1cb493cc8be2f1f6).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block A_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance A_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*nb*nblocks**B**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). Contains the blocks B_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a114ea0d398c1940f1cb493cc8be2f1f6).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_{li}.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use case is strideB >= ldb*nb*nblocks**C**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). Contains the blocks C_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_STRIDED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a114ea0d398c1940f1cb493cc8be2f1f6).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_{li}.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block C_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance C_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use case is strideC >= ldc*nb*nblocks**X**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideX). On entry, X contains the right-hand-side blocks R_{li}. It is overwritten by solution vectors X_{li} on exit.**ldx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldx >= nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks X_{li}.**strideX**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block X_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance X_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideX. Normal use case is strideX >= ldx*nblocks*nrhs**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dgeblttrs_npvt_interleaved_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, double *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incc, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC, double *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideX, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv444rocsolver_dgeblttrs_npvt_interleaved_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_interleaved_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nblocks, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)nrhs, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)inca, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, float *C, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incc, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldc, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideC, float *X, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)incx, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldx, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideX, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv444rocsolver_sgeblttrs_npvt_interleaved_batched14rocblas_handleK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideK11rocblas_int) GEBLTTRS_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED solves a batch of system of linear equations given by block tridiagonal matrices in its factorized form (without partial pivoting).

Each linear system has the form

\[\begin{split} M_lX_l = \left[\begin{array}{ccccc} B_{l1} & C_{ll}\\ A_{l1} & B_{ll} & C_{ll}\\ & \ddots & \ddots & \ddots \\ & & A_{l(n-2)} & B_{l(n-1)} & C_{l(n-1)}\\ & & & A_{l(n-1)} & B_{ln} \end{array}\right]\left[\begin{array}{c} X_{l1}\\ X_{l2}\\ X_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ X_{ln} \end{array}\right]=\left[\begin{array}{c} R_{l1}\\ R_{l2}\\ R_{l3}\\ \vdots\\ R_{ln} \end{array}\right]=R_l \end{split}\]where matrix \(M_l\) has \(n = \mathrm{nblocks}\) diagonal blocks of size nb, and the right-hand-side blocks \(R_{li}\) are general blocks of size nb-by-nrhs. The blocks of matrix \(M_l\) should be in the factorized form as returned by

[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a4213edac74a54c0dce60f49786fe0366).- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**nb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nb >= 0. The number of rows and columns of each block.**nblocks**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nblocks >= 0. The number of blocks along the diagonal of each matrix in the batch.**nrhs**–**[in]**rocblas_int. nrhs >= 0. The number of right hand sides, i.e., the number of columns of blocks R_{li}.**A**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). Contains the blocks A_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a4213edac74a54c0dce60f49786fe0366).**inca**–**[in]**rocblas_int. inca > 0. Stride from the start of one row of A_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are inca = 1 (strided batched case) or inca = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= inca * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks A_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of A_{li} to the next.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block A_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance A_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use cases are strideA >= lda*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideA = 1 (interleaved batched case).**B**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). Contains the blocks B_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a4213edac74a54c0dce60f49786fe0366).**incb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incb > 0. Stride from the start of one row of B_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are incb = 1 (strided batched case) or incb = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= incb * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks B_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of B_{li} to the next.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block B_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance B_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use cases are strideB >= ldb*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideB = 1 (interleaved batched case).**C**–**[in]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideC). Contains the blocks C_{li} as returned by[GEBLTTRF_NPVT_INTERLEAVED_BATCHED](#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a4213edac74a54c0dce60f49786fe0366).**incc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incc > 0. Stride from the start of one row of C_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are incc = 1 (strided batched case) or incc = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**ldc**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldc >= incc * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks C_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of C_{li} to the next.**strideC**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block C_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance C_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideC. Normal use cases are strideC >= ldc*nb*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideC = 1 (interleaved batched case).**X**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideX). On entry, X contains the right-hand-side blocks R_{li}. It is overwritten by solution vectors X_{li} on exit.**incx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. incx > 0. Stride from the start of one row of X_{li} to the next. Normal use cases are incx = 1 (strided batched case) or incx = batch_count (interleaved batched case).**ldx**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldx >= incx * nb. Specifies the leading dimension of blocks X_{li}, i.e. the stride from the start of one column of X_{li} to the next.**strideX**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one block X_{li} to the same block in the next batch instance X_{(l+1)i}. There is no restriction for the value of strideX. Normal use cases are strideX >= ldx*nrhs*nblocks (strided batched case) or strideX = 1 (interleaved batched case).**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



## Symmetric eigensolvers[#](#symmetric-eigensolvers)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dsyevj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_ssyevj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) SYEVJ computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a real symmetric matrix A.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V\) as

\[ A^{(k)} = V' A^{(k-1)} V \]such that \(off(A^{(k)}) < off(A^{(k-1)})\), where \(A^{(0)} = A\) and \(off(A^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A^{(k)}\). As \(off(A^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If esort is rocblas_esort_ascending, then the eigenvalues are sorted and returned in ascending order. If esort is rocblas_esort_none, then the order of the returned eigenvalues is unspecified.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the eigenvectors of A if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once off(A) is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of A (i.e. off(A)) at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The eigenvalues of A in increasing order.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_dsyevj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_ssyevj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYEVJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of real symmetric matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A_l\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V_l\) as

\[ A_l^{(k)} = V_l' A_l^{(k-1)} V_l^{} \]such that \(off(A_l^{(k)}) < off(A_l^{(k-1)})\), where \(A_l^{(0)} = A_l\) and \(off(A_l^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\). As \(off(A_l^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A_l\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If esort is rocblas_esort_ascending, then the eigenvalues are sorted and returned in ascending order. If esort is rocblas_esort_none, then the order of the returned eigenvalues is unspecified.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once off(A_l) is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of A_l (i.e. off(A_l)) at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The eigenvalues of A_l in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_dsyevj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_ssyevj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYEVJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of real symmetric matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A_l\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V_l\) as

\[ A_l^{(k)} = V_l' A_l^{(k-1)} V_l^{} \]such that \(off(A_l^{(k)}) < off(A_l^{(k-1)})\), where \(A_l^{(0)} = A_l\) and \(off(A_l^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\). As \(off(A_l^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A_l\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If esort is rocblas_esort_ascending, then the eigenvalues are sorted and returned in ascending order. If esort is rocblas_esort_none, then the order of the returned eigenvalues is unspecified.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once off(A_l) is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of A_l (i.e. off(A_l)) at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The eigenvalues of A_l in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zheevj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zheevj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_cheevj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) HEEVJ computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a complex Hermitian matrix A.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V\) as

\[ A^{(k)} = V' A^{(k-1)} V \]such that \(off(A^{(k)}) < off(A^{(k-1)})\), where \(A^{(0)} = A\) and \(off(A^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A^{(k)}\). As \(off(A^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If esort is rocblas_esort_ascending, then the eigenvalues are sorted and returned in ascending order. If esort is rocblas_esort_none, then the order of the returned eigenvalues is unspecified.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the Hermitian matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the eigenvectors of A if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once off(A) is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of A (i.e. off(A)) at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The eigenvalues of A in increasing order.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zheevj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_zheevj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_cheevj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEEVJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of complex Hermitian matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A_l\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V_l\) as

\[ A_l^{(k)} = V_l' A_l^{(k-1)} V_l^{} \]such that \(off(A_l^{(k)}) < off(A_l^{(k-1)})\), where \(A_l^{(0)} = A_l\) and \(off(A_l^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\). As \(off(A_l^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A_l\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zheevj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_zheevj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_esort](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_esort)esort, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_cheevj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_esortK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEEVJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of complex Hermitian matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in an order depending on the value of esort. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

At the \(k\)-th iteration (or “sweep”), \(A_l\) is transformed by a product of Jacobi rotations \(V_l\) as

\[ A_l^{(k)} = V_l' A_l^{(k-1)} V_l^{} \]such that \(off(A_l^{(k)}) < off(A_l^{(k-1)})\), where \(A_l^{(0)} = A_l\) and \(off(A_l^{(k)})\) is the Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\). As \(off(A_l^{(k)}) \rightarrow 0\), the diagonal elements of \(A_l^{(k)}\) increasingly resemble the eigenvalues of \(A_l\).

Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**esort**–**[in]**[rocblas_esort](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a35374a9ef1c1cb404e9d8daddb866901). Specifies the order of the returned eigenvalues. If esort is rocblas_esort_ascending, then the eigenvalues are sorted and returned in ascending order. If esort is rocblas_esort_none, then the order of the returned eigenvalues is unspecified.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the Hermitian matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are unchanged.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once off(A_l) is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements of A_l (i.e. off(A_l)) at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The eigenvalues of A_l in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_dsygvj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_ssygvj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) SYGVJ computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^T B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^T B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the symmetric matrix A. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrix A (including the diagonal) is destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.
