[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_dsygvj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_ssygvj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^T B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^T B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the symmetric matrices A_l. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z_l of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrices A_l (including the diagonal) are destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A_l.**B**–**[out]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration for each batch instance.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch instance l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, -
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_ssygvj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^T B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^T B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the symmetric matrices A_l. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z_l of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrices A_l (including the diagonal) are destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use is strideA >= lda*n.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a62177c8dae1549385502c300b7a4724a).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix B_l to the next one B_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use is strideB >= ldb*n.**abstol**–**[in]**type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration for each batch instance.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zhegvj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const double abstol, double *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, double *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_zhegvj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intKdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv416rocsolver_chegvj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) HEGVJ computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^H B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^H B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]Note

In order to carry out calculations, this method may synchronize the stream contained within the rocblas_handle.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the hermitian matrix A. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrix A (including the diagonal) is destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the hermitian positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv424rocsolver_chegvj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a batch of complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^H B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^H B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the hermitian matrices A_l. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z_l of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrices A_l (including the diagonal) are destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A_l.**B**–**[out]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the hermitian positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration for each batch instance.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zhegvj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, const float abstol, float *residual, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)max_sweeps,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*n_sweeps, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv432rocsolver_chegvj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a batch of complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^H B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^H B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the hermitian matrices A_l. On exit, if evect is original, the normalized matrix Z_l of eigenvectors. If evect is none, then the upper or lower triangular part of the matrices A_l (including the diagonal) are destroyed, depending on the value of uplo.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use is strideA >= lda*n.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). On entry, the hermitian positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a62177c8dae1549385502c300b7a4724a).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix B_l to the next one B_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use is strideB >= ldb*n.**abstol**–**[in]**real type. The absolute tolerance. The algorithm is considered to have converged once the residual is <= abstol. If abstol <= 0, then the tolerance will be set to machine precision.**residual**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array of batch_count scalars on the GPU. The Frobenius norm of the off-diagonal elements at the final iteration for each batch instance.**max_sweeps**–**[in]**rocblas_int. max_sweeps > 0. Maximum number of sweeps (iterations) to be used by the algorithm.**n_sweeps**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The actual number of sweeps (iterations) used by the algorithm for each batch instance.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). On exit, the eigenvalues in increasing order.**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use is strideW >= n.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_dsyevdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_ssyevdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) SYEVDJ computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a real symmetric matrix A.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A.

**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the eigenvectors of A if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n.

The eigenvalues of A in increasing order.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU.

If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_dsyevdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_ssyevdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYEVDJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of real symmetric matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

The eigenvalues of A_l in increasing order.

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one vector D_l to the next one D_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideD. Normal use case is strideD >= n.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU.

If info[l] = 0, successful exit for A_l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge for A_l.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_dsyevdj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_ssyevdj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYEVDJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and optionally the eigenvectors of a batch of real symmetric matrices A_l.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**Pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA).

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the eigenvectors of A_l if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.

**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

The eigenvalues of A_l in increasing order.

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one vector D_l to the next one D_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideD. Normal use case is strideD >= n.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU.

If info[l] = 0, successful exit for A_l. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge for A_l.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

Number of matrices in the batch.

The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach depending on the value of evect. The computed eigenvectors are orthonormal.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_dsygvdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_ssygvdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) SYGVDJ computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^T B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^T B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8).

Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.

**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A.

**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the normalized matrix Z of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.

**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n.

On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by

[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrix B.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n.

The eigenvalues in increasing order.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU.

If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.




-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_dsygvdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_ssygvdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVDJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z_l of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^T_l B_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^T_l B^{-1}_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8).

Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.

**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the normalized matrices Z_l of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.

**B**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n.

On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by

[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices B_l.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

The eigenvalues in increasing order.

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one vector D_l to the next one D_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideD. Normal use is strideD >= n.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU.

If info[l] = 0, successful exit. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge for matrix A_l. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

Number of eigenproblems in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_dsygvdj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, float *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_ssygvdj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVDJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^T_l B_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^T_l B^{-1}_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA).

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the normalized matrices Z_l of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB).

[POTRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a62177c8dae1549385502c300b7a4724a).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zhegvdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_zhegvdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intP22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intPdP11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdj([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *D,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_chegvdj14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intPfP11rocblas_int) HEGVDJ computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of a complex generalized Hermitian-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^H B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^H B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8).

Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.

**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A.

**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the normalized matrix Z of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.

**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n.

On entry, the Hermitian positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by

[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrix B.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n.

The eigenvalues in increasing order.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU.

If info = 0, successful exit. If info = 1, the algorithm did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zhegvdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_zhegvdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC22rocblas_double_complexK11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdj_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, float *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_chegvdj_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVDJ_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of batch of complex generalized Hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z_l of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^H_l B_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^H_l B^{-1}_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8).

Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.

**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n.

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the normalized matrices Z_l of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.

**B**–**[inout]**array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n.

On entry, the Hermitian positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by

[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices B_l.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

The eigenvalues in increasing order.

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one vector D_l to the next one D_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideD. Normal use is strideD >= n.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU.

If info[l] = 0, successful exit. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge for matrix A_l. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

Number of eigenproblems in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zhegvdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA,[rocblas_double_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv422rocblas_double_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, double *D, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideD,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdj_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,
