const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_chegvdj_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVDJ_STRIDED_BATCHED computes the eigenvalues and (optionally) eigenvectors of batch of complex generalized Hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvalues are found using the iterative Jacobi algorithm, and are returned in ascending order. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer algorithm, depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z_l of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^H_l B_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^H_l B^{-1}_l Z_l=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8).

Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.

**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2).

Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.

**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill.

Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.

**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0.

Number of rows and columns of matrix A_l.

**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA).

On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the normalized matrices Z_l of eigenvectors if they were computed and the algorithm converged; otherwise the contents of A_l are destroyed.

**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.

**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use is strideA >= lda*n.

**B**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB).

On entry, the Hermitian positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by

[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n.

Specifies the leading dimension of matrices B_l.

**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one matrix B_l to the next one B_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use is strideB >= ldb*n.

**D**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideD).

The eigenvalues in increasing order.

**strideD**–**[in]**rocblas_stride.

Stride from the start of one vector D_l to the next one D_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideD. Normal use is strideD >= n.

**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU.

If info[l] = 0, successful exit. If info[l] = 1, the algorithm did not converge for matrix A_l. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.

**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0.

Number of eigenproblems in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W, double *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_dsyevdx14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, float *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_ssyevdx14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) SYEVDX computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a real symmetric matrix A.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of A, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the contents of A are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**vl**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The first nev elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info = 0, the first nev columns contain the eigenvectors of A corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix Z.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, the algorithm did not converge. i columns of Z did not converge.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, double *const Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_dsyevdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideA_PCdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, float *const Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_ssyevdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYEVDX_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of real symmetric matrices A_l.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of A_l, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the contents of A_l are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**vl**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev[l]. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, the algorithm did not converge. i columns of Z_l did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsyevdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, double *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_dsyevdx_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_stridePdK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssyevdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, HEEVDX computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a Hermitian matrix A.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of A, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrix A is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrix A.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the contents of A are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**vl**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The first nev elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info = 0, the first nev columns contain the eigenvectors of A corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix Z.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i > 0, the algorithm did not converge. i columns of Z did not converge.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_zheevdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, [rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*const Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_cheevdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEEVDX_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of Hermitian matrices A_l.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of A_l, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower part of the symmetric matrices A_l is stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) part of A_l is not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. Number of rows and columns of matrices A_l.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the contents of A_l are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**vl**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev[l]. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, the algorithm did not converge. i columns of Z_l did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_cheevdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, HEEVDX_STRIDED_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of Hermitian matrices A_l.

This function computes all the eigenvalues of A_l, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideZ). On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**strideZ**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit for matrix A_l. If info[l] = i > 0, the algorithm did not converge. i columns of Z_l did not converge.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, double *W, double *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_dsygvdx14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intPdK11rocblas_intKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdPdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, float *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_ssygvdx14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfPfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) SYGVDX computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^T B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^T B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the contents of A are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B.**vl**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The first nev elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info = 0, the first nev columns contain the eigenvectors of A corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix Z.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i <= n, i columns of Z did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, double *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, double *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const double vl, const double vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, double *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, double *const Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_dsygvdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intA_PCdK11rocblas_intKdKdK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPdK14rocblas_strideA_PCdK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int)

-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *const A[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, float *const B[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, float *const Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_ssygvdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intA_PCfK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideA_PCfK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVDX_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^T B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^T B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the contents of A_l are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**B**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**vl**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev[l]. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch instance l. If info[l] = i <= n, i columns of Z_l did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.



-
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_dsygvdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, -
[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_ssygvdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n, float *A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideA, float *B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideB, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideW, float *Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz, const[rocblas_stride](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_stride)strideZ,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_ssygvdx_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intPfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_stridePfK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) SYGVDX_STRIDED_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of real generalized symmetric-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^T B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^T B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideA). On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the contents of A_l are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**strideA**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix A_l to the next one A_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideA. Normal use case is strideA >= lda*n.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideB). On entry, the symmetric positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_STRIDED_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a62177c8dae1549385502c300b7a4724a).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**strideB**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix B_l to the next one B_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideB. Normal use is strideB >= ldb*n.**vl**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideZ). On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**strideZ**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one matrix Z_l to the next one Z_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideZ. Normal use case is strideZ >= ldz*nev[l]. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch l. If info[l] = i <= n, i columns of Z_l did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdx([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_eform](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_eform)itype, const[rocblas_evect](types.html#_CPPv413rocblas_evect)evect, const[rocblas_erange](types.html#_CPPv414rocblas_erange)erange, const[rocblas_fill](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv412rocblas_fill)uplo, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)n,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*A, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)lda,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*B, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldb, const float vl, const float vu, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)il, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)iu,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*nev, float *W,[rocblas_float_complex](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv421rocblas_float_complex)*Z, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info)[#](#_CPPv417rocsolver_chegvdx14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_int) HEGVDX computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblem.

The problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A X = \lambda B X & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A B X = \lambda X & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B A X = \lambda X & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix Z of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z^H B Z=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z^H B^{-1} Z=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblem.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A and B are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A and B are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrix A. On exit, the contents of A are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix A.**B**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the hermitian positive definite matrix B. On exit, the triangular factor of B as returned by[POTRF](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a33f3fbe51b637b25d59a4507ae43221f).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B.**vl**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU of dimension n. The first nev elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**Z**–**[out]**pointer to type. Array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info = 0, the first nev columns contain the eigenvectors of A corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrix Z.**info**–**[out]**pointer to a rocblas_int on the GPU. If info = 0, successful exit. If info = i <= n, i columns of Z did not converge. If info = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B is not positive definite.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdx_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, Z[], const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)ldz,[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)*info, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv425rocsolver_chegvdx_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideA_PC21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVDX_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^H B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^H B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

- Parameters:
**handle**–**[in]**rocblas_handle.**itype**–**[in]**[rocblas_eform](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a1dd267d37dbe5c1b6e5edeb7996beda8). Specifies the form of the generalized eigenproblems.**evect**–**[in]**[rocblas_evect](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a4a490507ad978c2dfffe8991d940d8a2). Specifies whether the eigenvectors are to be computed. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, then the eigenvectors are computed. rocblas_evect_tridiagonal is not supported.**erange**–**[in]**[rocblas_erange](types.html#rocsolver-extra-types_8h_1a477116663c5b6a6fa865544fdfca9981). Specifies the type of range or interval of the eigenvalues to be computed.**uplo**–**[in]**rocblas_fill. Specifies whether the upper or lower parts of the matrices A_l and B_l are stored. If uplo indicates lower (or upper), then the upper (or lower) parts of A_l and B_l are not used.**n**–**[in]**rocblas_int. n >= 0. The matrix dimensions.**A**–**[inout]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension lda*n. On entry, the matrices A_l. On exit, the contents of A_l are destroyed.**lda**–**[in]**rocblas_int. lda >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices A_l.**B**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldb*n. On entry, the hermitian positive definite matrices B_l. On exit, the triangular factor of B_l as returned by[POTRF_BATCHED](lapack.html#rocsolver-functions_8h_1a64637bff034365c2667eca3721eff4a9).**ldb**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldb >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of B_l.**vl**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The lower bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**vu**–**[in]**real type. vl < vu. The upper bound of the search interval (vl, vu]. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues within a set of indices.**il**–**[in]**rocblas_int. il = 1 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise. The index of the smallest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**iu**–**[in]**rocblas_int. iu = 0 if n = 0; 1 <= il <= iu otherwise.. The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed. Ignored if range indicates to look for all the eigenvalues of A_l or the eigenvalues in a half-open interval.**nev**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. The total number of eigenvalues found. If erange is rocblas_erange_all, nev[l] = n. If erange is rocblas_erange_index, nev[l] = iu - il + 1. Otherwise, 0 <= nev[l] <= n.**W**–**[out]**pointer to real type. Array on the GPU (the size depends on the value of strideW). The first nev[l] elements contain the computed eigenvalues. (The remaining elements can be used as workspace for internal computations).**strideW**–**[in]**rocblas_stride. Stride from the start of one vector W_l to the next one W_(l+1). There is no restriction for the value of strideW. Normal use case is strideW >= n.**Z**–**[out]**Array of pointers to type. Each pointer points to an array on the GPU of dimension ldz*nev[l]. On exit, if evect is not rocblas_evect_none and info[l] = 0, the first nev[l] columns contain the eigenvectors of A_l corresponding to the output eigenvalues. Not referenced if evect is rocblas_evect_none. Note: If erange is rocblas_range_value, then the values of nev[l] are not known in advance. The user should ensure that Z_l is large enough to hold n columns, as all n columns can be used as workspace for internal computations.**ldz**–**[in]**rocblas_int. ldz >= n. Specifies the leading dimension of matrices Z_l.**info**–**[out]**pointer to rocblas_int. Array of batch_count integers on the GPU. If info[l] = 0, successful exit of batch instance l. If info[l] = i <= n, i columns of Z_l did not converge. If info[l] = n + i, the leading minor of order i of B_l is not positive definite.**batch_count**–**[in]**rocblas_int. batch_count >= 0. Number of matrices in the batch.

[rocblas_status](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/enumerations.html#_CPPv414rocblas_status)rocsolver_chegvdx_strided_batched([rocblas_handle](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv414rocblas_handle)handle, const[rocblas_int](https://rocm.docs.amd.com/projects/rocBLAS/en/latest/reference/datatypes.html#_CPPv411rocblas_int)batch_count)[#](#_CPPv433rocsolver_chegvdx_strided_batched14rocblas_handleK13rocblas_eformK13rocblas_evectK14rocblas_erangeK12rocblas_fillK11rocblas_intP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideKfKfK11rocblas_intK11rocblas_intP11rocblas_intPfK14rocblas_strideP21rocblas_float_complexK11rocblas_intK14rocblas_strideP11rocblas_intK11rocblas_int) HEGVDX_STRIDED_BATCHED computes a set of the eigenvalues and optionally the corresponding eigenvectors of a batch of complex generalized hermitian-definite eigenproblems.

For each instance in the batch, the problem solved by this function is either of the form

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} A_l X_l = \lambda B_l X_l & \: \text{1st form,}\\ A_l B_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{2nd form, or}\\ B_l A_l X_l = \lambda X_l & \: \text{3rd form,} \end{array} \end{split}\]depending on the value of itype. The eigenvectors are computed depending on the value of evect.

When computed, the matrix \(Z_l\) of eigenvectors is normalized as follows:

\[\begin{split} \begin{array}{cl} Z_l^H B_l^{} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 1st or 2nd form, or}\\ Z_l^H B_l^{-1} Z_l^{}=I & \: \text{if 3rd form.} \end{array} \end{split}\]This function computes all the eigenvalues, all the eigenvalues in the half-open interval \((vl, vu]\), or the il-th through iu-th eigenvalues, depending on the value of erange. If evect is rocblas_evect_original, the eigenvectors for these eigenvalues will be computed as well. The eigenvectors are computed using a divide-and-conquer approach.

The index of the largest eigenvalue to be computed.
